# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 07:49:25.710167

### Base Program

```py
def replaceElements(arr):
    n = len(arr)
    maxElement = -1
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        temp = arr[i]
        arr[i] = maxElement
        maxElement = max(maxElement, temp)
    return arr
```

## Test Case 1

        arr[i] = maxElement
        maxElement = max(maxElement, temp)
    return arr

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py

def replaceElements(arr):
    n = len(arr)
    maxElement = -1
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        temp = arr[i]
        arr[i] = maxElement
        maxElement = max(maxElement, temp)
    return arr


```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py

def replaceElements(arr):
    n = len(arr)
    maxElement = -1
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        temp = arr[i]
        arr[i] = maxElement
        maxElement = max(maxElement, temp)
    return arr


```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py

def replaceElements(arr):
    n = len(arr)
    maxElement = -1
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        temp = arr[i]
        arr[i] = maxElement
        maxElement = max(maxElement, temp)
    return arr


```

## Test Case 5

### Modified Program

```py

def replaceElements(arr):
    n = len(arr)
    maxElement = -1
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        temp = arr[i]
        arr[i] = maxElement
        maxElement = max(maxElement, temp)
    return arr


```

## Test Case 6

### Modified Program

```py

def replaceElements(arr):
    n = len(arr)
    maxElement = -1
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        temp = arr[i]
        arr[i] = maxElement
        maxElement = max(maxElement, temp)
    return arr


```

## Test Case 7

### Modified Program

```py

def replaceElements(arr):
    n = len(arr)
    maxElement = -1
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        temp = arr[i]
        arr[i] = maxElement
        maxElement = max(maxElement, temp)
    return arr


```

## Test Case 8

### Modified Program

```py

def replaceElements(arr):
    n = len(arr)
    maxElement = -1
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        temp = arr[i]
        arr[i] = maxElement
        maxElement = max(maxElement, temp)
    return arr


```

## Test Case 9

### Modified Program

```py

def replaceElements(arr):
    n = len(arr)
    maxElement = -1
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        temp = arr[i]
        arr[i] = maxElement
        maxElement = max(maxElement, temp)
    return arr


```

## Test Case 10

### Modified Program

```py

def replaceElements(arr):
    n = len(arr)
    maxElement = -1
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        temp = arr[i]
        arr[i] = maxElement
        maxElement = max(maxElement, temp)
    return arr


```
